=== b'Requirements for Verification' ===

b'Requirements for Verification\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThe blue Verified badge\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n on Twitter lets people know that an account of public interest is authentic. To receive the blue badge, your account must be authentic,\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0notable, and active.\n\n\n\n\n\n\nAuthentic\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nTo encourage and maintain trust between users on the platform, you will need to confirm your identity with Twitter in order to be Verified. Depending on the category, you will be asked to choose one of the following three methods of verifying your identity:\n\n\n\n\nOfficial website: Provide the link to an official website that references you (or your organization) and your Twitter account. For individuals, the organization that owns the website must be Verified on Twitter.ID verification: Provide a photo of a valid official government-issued identification document, such as your Driver\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s License or Passport. This requirement applies to individuals, not companies, brands, or organizations.Official email address: Provide an official email address with a domain relevant to the notability category you choose. For individuals, the organization the domain is associated with must be Verified on Twitter.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nNotable\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYour account must represent or otherwise be associated with a prominently recognized individual or brand, in line with the notability criteria described below. In addition to confirming the identity of the controller of the account, Twitter will Verify the following types of accounts based on the criteria described. In all categories, Twitter may independently confirm qualifying affiliation through business partnerships or direct outreach. For each category we may request the following type of information to confirm notability:\n\n\n\n\nNews Coverage: Provide news articles that are about or reference yourself or your organization multiple times in the article. These articles must be from Verified news organizations and cannot be a blog or self-published content. Some categories may require you to submit articles that reference or link to your or your organization\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Twitter handle in addition to referring to you or your organization.Google Trends: Provide a link to a profile on Google Trends that depicts search history and is linked to the category in which you are applying.Wikipedia: Provide a link to a stable Wikipedia article about you or your organization that meets the encyclopedia\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s notability standards.Other industry specific references: Depending on the category, we may ask for more industry specific references such as a link to an IMDB page for entertainment.Follower or Mention Count: If your account is detected to be in the top .05% follower or mention count for your geographic location, it may count towards notability evidence for certain categories.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\nActive\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYour account must be active with a record of adherence to the Twitter Rules. This means:\n\n\n\n\nComplete: Your account must have a profile name, and a profile image;\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Active use: Your account must be public at the time of application and you must have logged into that account in the last six months;Security: Your account must have a confirmed email address or phone number; andTwitter Rules: Your account must not have had a 12-hour or 7-day lockout for violating the Twitter Rules in the past 12 months (excluding successful appeals).*\xc3\x82'


=== b'Requirements for Verification' ===

b'How to apply for Verification \n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n      How to apply for Verification\n    \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            Step 1\n          \n\nNavigate to your profile icon and open the main menu.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n            Step 2\n          \n\nSelect Settings and privacy.\n\n\n\n\n            Step 3\n          \n\nSelect Your account.\n\n\n\n\n            Step 4\n          \n\nSelect Account information. You may need to enter in your password to continue.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n            Step 5\n          \n\nUnder Verified, select Verification request.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0 Then scroll down and select Apply now.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            Step 1\n          \n\nNavigate to your profile icon and open the main menu.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n            Step 2\n          \n\nSelect Settings and privacy.\n\n\n\n\n            Step 3\n          \n\nSelect Your account.\n\n\n\n\n            Step 4\n          \n\nSelect Account information. You may need to enter in your password to continue.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n            Step 5\n          \n\nUnder Verified, select Verification request.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0 Then scroll down and select Apply now.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            Step 1\n          \n\nNavigate to more\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n icon in the main menu.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n            Step 2\n          \n\nSelect Settings and Support.\n\n\n\n\n            Step 3\n          \n\nSelect\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Settings and Privacy.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n            Step 4\n          \n\nSelect Your account.\n\n\n\n\n            Step 5\n          \n\nSelect Account information. Enter in your password to continue.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n            Step 6\n          \n\nUnder Verified, select Request Verification.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0 Then Start request.\xc3\x82'


=== b'Requirements for Verification' ===

b"Categories for Verification\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThe specific requirements for authenticity, notability and activity are outlined by category and subcategory below:\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\nGovernment\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nGovernment Office Accounts\n\nAccounts of current government agencies, departments/ministries, and institutions.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrerequisites:\n\n\n\n\n\nAccount includes a relevant link to an official government URL on their profileAccount must satisfy the criteria outlined in the above category denoting \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cactive\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d accounts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYou may also be required to provide the following information to determine your notability and authenticity:\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nLinks to at least 5 relevant articles that reference the applicant multiple times as a government office or public service\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nVerify an email address with an official government domainOfficial websites or news articles published by already Verified organizations that reference the organization\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Twitter handle or registered email address can help authenticate the applicant's account\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nIndividuals in Government\n\nAccounts of federal or state level government officials, such as, heads of state, elected officials, appointed ministers, ambassadors, and official spokespeople.\nPrerequisites:\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nAccount references their government position in their bioIs their official account for their office, not a personal or campaign account\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nAccount links official government URL on their profileAre currently serving in government office mentioned in their bioAccount must satisfy the criteria outlined in the above category denoting \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cactive\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d accounts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYou may also be required to provide the following information to determine your notability and authenticity:\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPublic reference to your name and Twitter handle on official site of a Verified government entity; URL must link to specific page of referenceLinks to at least 5 news articles that reference you in your government positionVerify an email address with an official government domainA photo of your valid government-issued ID\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nCandidates for Office\n\nAccounts of official candidates for state- or national-level public office in upcoming elections. Candidates will not qualify unless registered with the appropriate election authority.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrerequisites:\n\n\n\n\n\nAccount references that they are a candidate and what office they are running forAccount links to URL of campaign websiteIndividual is officially registered with the appropriate election authority in a state or national level public election that has not yet occurredAccount must satisfy the criteria outlined in the above category denoting \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cactive\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d accounts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYou may also be required to provide the following information to determine your notability and authenticity:\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nA link to your official campaign website, which also references your Twitter handleLinks to 5 news articles, published in the previous 6 months before applying, that reference you as a candidate for officeA photo of your valid government-issued IDOfficial websites or news articles published by already Verified organizations that reference your Twitter handle or registered email address can help authenticate the your account\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\nNews organizations, individuals in news & journalists\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nNews organizations\n\nAccounts of current government agencies, departments/ministries, and institutions.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrerequisites:\n\n\n\n\n\nYour account links to official website in bioYour account must satisfy the criteria outlined in the above category denoting \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cactive\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d accounts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYou may also be required to provide the following information to determine your notability and authenticity:\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nA link to an official website that references your organization and your Twitter accountThe account demonstrates sufficient platform presence in the top .05% of active accounts located in the same geographic regionThe account demonstrates a public presence by providing Google Trends evidence, link to a stable Wikipedia article that meets the encyclopedia\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s notability standards, or listing on a qualifying stock exchangeLinks to 3 articles referencing the applicant as a news organization published by a Verified organization within the last 6 monthsOfficial websites or news articles published by already Verified organizations that reference the applicant\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Twitter handle or registered email address can help authenticate the applicant's account\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nIndividuals in news\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\nAccounts of individuals employed by Verified news organizations in a public-facing news reporting role including reporters, news anchors, and editors.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrerequisites:\n\n\n\n\n\nYour account must refer directly to the name and official URL of the qualifying organization in your Twitter bio. (Either @mention or include URL to your employer\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s official site)Your employer already has a Verified accountYour account must satisfy the criteria outlined in the above category denoting \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cactive\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d accounts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYou may also be required to provide the following information to determine your notability and authenticity:\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nEvidence that you and your Twitter handle is listed on official company websiteLinks to 3 articles crediting you as an author published by your employer published within the last 6 monthsA photo of your valid government-issued IDOfficial websites or news articles published by already Verified organizations that reference the applicant\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Twitter handle or registered email address can help authenticate your account\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFreelance Journalists\n\nIndividuals who are not employed by, but consistently publish in Verified news publications.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrerequisite:\n\n\n\n\n\nYour account must satisfy the criteria outlined in the above category denoting active accounts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYou may also be required to provide the following information to determine your notability and authenticity:\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nLinks to 3 articles crediting you as the author from an already Verified news organization within the past 6 months. Opinion pieces will not be accepted.A photo of your valid government-issued IDOfficial websites or news articles published by already Verified organizations that reference the applicant\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Twitter handle or registered email address can help authenticate your account\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\nCompanies, brands & organizations\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nOrganizations\nAccounts representing prominent organizations including companies, brands, non-profit organizations. Secondary affiliated accounts of Verified organizations may also qualify.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrerequisites:\n\n\n\n\n\nAccount links to their official company website in their profileAccount must satisfy the criteria outlined in the above category denoting active accounts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYou may also be required to provide the following information to determine your notability and authenticity:\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nA link to a website that demonstrates your organization\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s presence in a public stock exchangeA link to a stable Wikipedia article about your organization that meets the encyclopedia\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s notability standardsLinks to 3 or more news articles about your organization published by an already Verified news organization within the 6 months prior to applyingDemonstrate your account has a follower count in the top .05% of active accounts located in the same geographic region\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nLeaders & Executives\n\nLeaders and other prominent executives of Verified companies, brands and non-profit organizations.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrerequisite:\n\n\n\n\n\nAccount must satisfy the criteria outlined in the above category denoting active accounts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYou may also be required to provide the following information to determine your notability and authenticity:\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nA link to your organization website that references individual and Twitter accountA link to a stable Wikipedia article about you that meet the encyclopedia\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s notability standardsLinks to 3 or more news articles referencing you in a leadership position published by a Verified news organization within the 6 months prior to applyingA photo of your valid government-issued ID\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\nEntertainment\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nEntertainment or Production Company\nAccounts of major entertainment companies, such as film studios, TV networks, and music entities may be Verified. Official accounts of productions associated with these entities, such as films, events/festivals, or TV shows, may be Verified as long as they are affiliated with a Verified entertainment organization.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrerequisites:\n\n\n\n\n\nProfile links to official websiteAccount must satisfy the criteria outlined in the above category denoting active accounts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYou may also be required to provide the following information to determine your notability and authenticity:\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nDemonstrate sufficient platform presence in the top .05% of active accounts located in the same geographic regionDemonstrate a public presence by providing Google Trends evidence, link to a stable Wikipedia article that meet the encyclopedia\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s notability standards, or listing on a qualifying stock exchangeLinks to 3 or more news articles about the organization published by a Verified news organization within the 6 months prior to applyingA link to the organization\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s official websiteOfficial websites or news articles published by already Verified organizations that reference the applicant\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Twitter handle or registered email address can help authenticate the applicant's account\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nIndividual in entertainment\n\nIndividual accounts of artists, performers, directors, and others in similar public-facing roles associated with such entities or their productions.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrerequisites:\n\n\n\n\n\nProfile links to official website of Verified entertainment entity referencing applicant provided as notability evidenceAccount must satisfy the criteria outlined in the above category denoting active accounts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYou may also be required to provide the following information to determine your notability and authenticity:\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nA link to the applicant's IMDB page containing 50+ production creditsLinks to 3 articles featuring applicant from Verified news publishers within the last 6 monthsA link to a website that specifically reference applicant\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Twitter account and is the website of an official site of an already Verified organizationA photo of a valid government-issued IDOfficial websites or news articles published by already Verified organizations that reference the applicant\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Twitter handle or registered email address can help authenticate the applicant's account\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\nSports & gaming\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nProfessional sport organizations, teams & leagues\nAccounts of professional sports leagues, clubs, teams and global competitions such as Olympics and Paralympics.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrerequisites:\n\n\n\n\n\nAccount links to their official company website in their profileAccount must satisfy the criteria outlined in the above category denoting active accounts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYou may also be required to provide the following information to determine your notability and authenticity:\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nDemonstrate sufficient platform presence in the top .05% of active accounts located in the same geographic regionA link to an already Verified official sports organization, team, or league website that references the applicantDemonstrate a public presence by providing Google Trends evidence, link to a stable Wikipedia article that meets the encyclopedia\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s notability standards, or listing on a qualifying stock exchangeLinks to 3 or more news articles about the organization published by Verified news organization within the 6 months prior to applyingOfficial websites or news articles published by already Verified organizations that reference the applicant\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Twitter handle or registered email address can help authenticate the applicant's account\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nIndividuals in professional sports\n\nIndividual accounts of athletes, coaches, team members, and others in similar management or public-facing roles associated with such entities.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nNote: We will not Verify amateur athletes who compete at the collegiate level (or lower) nor in official minor leagues unless they meet the criteria for Verification under the influential individuals category.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrerequisite:\n\n\n\n\n\nAccount must satisfy the criteria outlined in the above category denoting active accounts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYou may also be required to provide the following information to determine your notability and authenticity:\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nA link to a website that specifically references applicant and is the official site of an already Verified organizationLinks to 3 or more articles featuring the applicant as a professional individual in sports published by Verified news organizations within 6 months prior to applyingA photo of a valid government-issued IDOfficial websites or news articles published by already Verified organizations that reference the applicant\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Twitter handle or registered email address can help authenticate the applicant's account\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nIndividuals in gaming\n\nIndividual accounts of esport athletes that are affiliated with Verified gaming teams or leagues.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrerequisites:\n\n\n\n\n\nAccount\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s follower count is in the top .05% in their regionAre affiliated with a Verified gaming team or league and reference it in their bioAccount must satisfy the criteria outlined in the above category denoting active accounts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYou may also be required to provide the following information to determine your notability and authenticity:\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nA link to official team or league website referencing applicant as professional esports athlete or coach for Verified esports teamLinks to 3 or more articles about or referencing the individual published within the 6 months prior to applying in news outlets such as Launcher, Gamesbeat, Dexerto, Kotaku, Polygon, or IGNA photo of a valid government-issued IDOfficial websites or news articles published by already Verified organizations that reference the applicant\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Twitter handle or registered email address can help authenticate the applicant's account\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\nActivists & organizers\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\nOutside the professional categories defined above, people who are using Twitter effectively to bring awareness, share information, and galvanize community members around a cause, to bring about socioeconomic, political, or cultural change, or to otherwise foster community, may be Verified.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrerequisites:\n\n\n\n\n\nAccount is reflecting an individual, not an organizationAccount\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s follower count is in the top .05% in their regionAccount must satisfy the criteria outlined in the above category denoting active accounts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYou may also be required to provide the following information to determine your notability and authenticity:\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nAn official website associated with advocacy work that references the account holder's name or indicates they hold a leadership position at the advocacy group.Links to 3 or more articles about the individual and their advocacy work published in a Verified news sources within the last 6 monthsOfficial websites or news articles published by already Verified organizations that reference the applicant\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Twitter handle or registered email address can help authenticate the applicant's account\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n*In response to current events, we may Verify accounts that do not fully meet the criteria above due to their expertise or public role in matters of high public interest, as well as their susceptibility to impersonation. For example:\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nMedical professionals during epidemics or other public health crises;Activists and local political leaders in times of protest or in connection with a significant cultural event;Public safety and journalist accounts reporting on natural disasters; orOrganizers, proponents, or founders of campaigns in support of civil or human rights\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\nContent creators & influential individuals\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nEstablished digital content creators who consistently publish original content (regardless of platform) for at least 6 months prior to applying and meet the follower or mention criteria listed below for other influential individuals.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrerequisites:\n\n\n\n\n\nAccount is reflecting an individual, not an organizationAccount meets criteria for significant platform presence (top .05% of mentions or follower count) in their geographic regionAccount must satisfy the criteria outlined in the above category denoting active accounts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nYou may also be required to provide the following information to determine your notability and authenticity:\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nA profile on Google Trends with evidence of recent search activityA stable Wikipedia article about you that meets the encyclopedia\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s notability standards for peopleLinks to 3 or more featured references within the 6 months prior to applying in news outlets that meet the News criteria above; including specialty publications related to your profession or expertiseA link to a content page outside of Twitter that shows your published content over the last 6 monthsOfficial websites or news articles published by already Verified organizations that reference the applicant\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Twitter handle or registered email address can help authenticate the applicant's account.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\xc3\x82"

=== b'Requirements for Verification' ===

b'Ineligible accounts\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nCertain accounts are ineligible for the blue badge, regardless of satisfying the requirements (authentic, notable, and active), including:\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nParody, newsfeed, commentary, and unofficial fan accounts;Pets and fictional characters, unless directly affiliated with a Verified Company, Brand, or Organization, or with a Verified entertainment productionAccounts engaged in severe violations of our Platform manipulation and spam policy, such as the buying and selling of followers and engagementAccounts of individuals or groups associated with coordinated harmful activity, or hateful content as defined in Twitter\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Ads Policies, or that have been found to have committed gross human rights violations by an international court/tribunal, or a fact-finding mission or commission of inquiry authorized by an international organization, may be ineligible for Verification \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93 even if their activity on Twitter doesn\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t violate the Twitter RulesAccounts that routinely post content that harasses, shames, or insults any individual or group\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x94especially on the basis of race, ethnicity, national origin, sexual orientation, gender identity, religious affiliation, age, disability, medical/genetic condition, status as a veteran, status as a refugee, or status as an immigrant\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x94or content that promotes the supremacy or interests of members of any group in a manner likely to be perceived as demeaning on the basis of these categories; andAccounts promoting sale of the Verification badge itself or offering unauthorized assistance with the application process**\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n          FAQ & Loss of Verified Status\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFAQ\n\n\nLoss of Verified status\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            FAQ\n          \n\n            Loss of Verified status\n          \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nWhat does Verification mean?\n\nThe blue Verified badge on Twitter lets people know that an account of public interest is authentic.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\nWho can be Verified on Twitter?\n\nTo be Verified, your account must be notable and active. The types of notable accounts we currently Verify are:\nGovernmentNews organizations, individuals in news & journalistsCompanies, brands & organizationsEntertainmentSports & gamingActivists & organizersContent creators & influential individuals\n\n\n\n\n\nCan anyone get Twitter Verified?\n\nAnyone can apply for Verification. Please read the requirements to understand if your account qualifies before you apply. Learn how to apply for verification.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\nHow can I get Verified on Twitter?\n\nFirst, make sure you meet the requirements\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0and\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0categories\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0for Verification. If your account satisfies the criteria, follow the steps on\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0how to apply for verification.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\nHow do I know if I am Verified?\n\nLook for the blue Verified badge on your Twitter profile. All Verified accounts have the badge next to their display name.\n\n\n\n\n\nHow do I know if someone else is Verified?\n\nVerified accounts on Twitter will have a blue check next to their display name throughout the app.\n\n\n\n\n\nCan a Verified badge be automatically removed from an account?\n\nYes, as part of our\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0policy, Verified badges may be automatically removed from inactive and incomplete accounts. A complete Twitter account is defined as one with all of the following elements:\neither a verified email address or phone numbera profile imagea display name\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nCan I request to remove my Verified badge?\n\nIt\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s not currently possible to request that Twitter remove your Verified badge.\n\n\n\n\n\nCan I request to remove another account\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Verified badge?\n\nIt\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s not currently possible to request that Twitter remove an account\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Verified badge.\n\n\n\n\n\nWhy might Twitter remove the Verified badge from an account?\n\nPlease see the next tab on Loss of Verified status.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nIn accordance with the Twitter Terms of Service, Twitter may remove the Verified status of an account at any time without notice.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nSometimes, changes made to an account by the owner may result in loss of Verified status. User-made changes include, but are not limited to:\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nIf you change your username (@handle)If your account becomes inactive or incompleteIf you are no longer in the position you initially were Verified for \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93 such as an elected government official who leaves office \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93 and you do not otherwise meet our criteria for VerificationIf changes to your account are misleading or substantially alter the persona present on your accountIf changes to your account result in failure to meet the eligibility requirements for Verification outlined aboveIf changes to your account cause you to fall under any of the categories in the "Ineligible Accounts" section\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nTwitter may also remove the blue badge from accounts that are found to be in severe or repeated violation of the Twitter Rules. Any violation of the Twitter Terms of Service or Twitter Rules, manipulation of Twitter processes, or circumvention of enforcement actions may result in loss of the badge or in certain instances, suspension. This includes:\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nImpersonation or intentionally misleading people on Twitter by changing your display name, bio, banner image, and/or profile image.Severe violations that result in immediate account suspension.Repeat policy violations in Tweets, including but not limited to:\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Hateful conductAbusive behaviorGlorification of violenceCivic integrity\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Private informationPlatform manipulation and spam\n\n\n\n\n\nRemoval of the badge based on repeated violations will be assessed on a case-by-case basis and is not automatic.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\nTwitter reserves the right to assess the qualifications of any Verified account under the currently published version of the Verification Policy.'

=== b'What does the blue checkmark mean?' ===

b'What does the blue checkmark mean?\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThe definition of verification and the accompanying blue checkmark is changing. Until now, Twitter used the blue checkmark to indicate active, notable, and authentic accounts of public interest that Twitter had independently verified based on\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0certain requirements.\n\n\n\n\nNow the blue checkmark may mean two different things: either that an account was verified under the previous verification criteria (active, notable, and authentic), or that the account has an active subscription to Twitter\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s new Twitter Blue subscription service, which was made available on iOS in the US, Canada, Australia New Zealand and the UK on November 9, 2022. Accounts that receive the blue checkmark as part of a Twitter Blue subscription will not undergo review to confirm that they meet the active, notable and authentic criteria that was used in the previous process.\n\n\n\n\nPlease note, to minimize impersonation risks, display name changes will be temporarily restricted on Verified accounts. This will impact accounts Verified under the legacy program and Twitter\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s new Twitter Blue subscription product.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n           Eligibility criteria\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nOnly accounts subscribed to Twitter Blue on iOS on or after November 9, 2022 are eligible for the blue checkmark moving forward.\nAs a result of this change, at this time, Twitter will no longer be accepting new applications for Verification under the previous criteria.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nNote that all accounts subscribed to Twitter Blue on iOS on or after November 9, 2022 will automatically receive a blue checkmark, which will persist for the duration of the subscribers\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99 subscription term.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n          Loss of the blue checkmark for Twitter Blue subscribers\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nTwitter Blue subscribers\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99 blue checkmarks may be taken away at any time for any reason at all by Twitter, including as the result of certain types of violations of the Twitter Rules, including but not limited to our rules around spam, ban evasion, and impersonation.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n          Loss of the blue checkmark for legacy verified accounts\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nLegacy verified accounts also may be taken away at any time for any reason at all by Twitter, including as the result of certain\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0 types of violations of the Twitter Rules, including but not limited to our rules around spam, ban evasion, and Impersonation. In addition, legacy verified accounts are still subject to the guidelines outlined in the \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cLoss of Verified Status\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d section of the previous policy.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n          What does the \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x98Official\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99 profile label mean?\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nIn addition to blue checkmarks, Twitter also applies visual identity signals like labels and badges on account profiles to provide more context about \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x94 and help distinguish \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x94 different types of accounts.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nThe Official profile label is applied to government accounts (institutional accounts, elected or appointed officials, and multilateral organizations)*, certain political organizations such as political parties, commercial companies including business partners, major brands, media outlets and publishers, and some other public figures.\n\n*State-affiliated media and government accounts that play a role as a geopolitical or official Government communication channel display a unique label. You can find more information about profile labels in our Help Center.\xc3\x82'


=== b'About locked accounts' ===

b'Verify your account by phone\n    \n\n\n\n\n\n\nLog in to your account. (If you don\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t have login access to your account, Contact our support team.)\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nLook for the message letting you know Your account has been locked.Select Start.Enter your phone number. Please note that we will associate this phone number with your account.We will send you a text message, or you will receive a phone call, with a verification code. It may take a few minutes for the code to be delivered to your phone.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Once you\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ve entered the verification code, click or tap Submit to unlock your account.\nIf you have an email address associated with your account, we also sent instructions to that address. If you don\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t see an email from us, please check your spam, junk and social folders.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n      Verify your account by email\n    \n\n\n\n\n\n\nLog in to your account. (If you don\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t have login access to your account, Contact our support team.)\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nLook for the message letting you know to verify your account.Select Start.On the next screen, select Send email to begin the verification process.Check your email inbox for an email from Twitter containing a verification code. It may take a few minutes for the code to be delivered to your email inbox.Once you\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ve entered the verification code, select Verify to unlock your account.\nIf you don\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t see an email from us, please check your spam, junk, and social folders.\nIf your account is in this state, people who visit your profile may see a message letting them know the account has displayed unusual activity and asking them to confirm they still want to view it.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n      Verify your account by recaptcha\n    \n\n\n\n\n\n\nIf your account appears to have exhibited automated behavior that violates the Twitter Rules, we may lock it and request that you pass a captcha challenge to confirm you are not a robot.\nLog in to your account. (If you don\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t have login access to your account, Contact our support team.)\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Look for the message letting you know to please verify your account.Select Start.You will see a pinwheel or wait cursor while the captcha check completes in the background. You do not need to do anything.Once we\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ve confirmed you are not a robot, select Continue to Twitter to unlock your account.\nIf you have an email address associated with your account, we also sent instructions to that address. If you don\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t see an email from us, please check your spam, junk and social folders.\nIf your account is in this state, people who visit your profile may see a message letting them know the account has displayed unusual activity and asking them to confirm they still want to view it.'

=== b'Community Notes and Twitter Rules' ===

b'Community Notes aim to create a better informed world by empowering people on Twitter to collaboratively add context to potentially misleading Tweets. Contributors can leave notes on any Tweet and if enough contributors from different points of view rate that note as helpful, the note will be publicly shown on a Tweet. Sign up to become a contributor.\nCommunity Notes are now publicly visible to everyone in the US. For more information, we have included responses to frequently asked questions below, but you can learn more through the Community Notes Guide as well.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nThis is an open and transparent process, that\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s why we\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ve made the\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Community Notes algorithm open source and publicly available on GitHub, along with the data that powers it so anyone can audit, analyze or suggest improvements.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n          Community Notes and Twitter Rules\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\nCommunity Notes do not represent Twitter\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s viewpoint and cannot be edited or modified by our teams. A Tweet with a\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Community Note will not be labeled, removed, or addressed by Twitter unless it is found to be violating the\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Twitter Rules, Terms of Service, or our Privacy Policy.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Failure to abide by the rules can result in one\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s removal from accessing Community Notes, and/or other remediations.\nAnyone can report notes they believe aren\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t in accordance with those rules by selecting the\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n menu on a note, and then selecting Report, or by using this form.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n      How to become a Community Notes contributor\n    \n\n\n\n\n\n\nLearn more about contributor eligibility and sign up here.\nWe plan to review applications on a rolling, periodic basis.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n      How to rate a Community Note\n    \n\n\n\n\n\n\nIf you see a Tweet with a Community Notes card and note, you can rate how helpful you think the note is.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nI have a note on my Tweet. What can I do?\nAs a Tweet author, if you disagree that a Community Note provides important context about your Tweet, you can\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0request additional review.'

=== b'Debunking Twitter myths' ===

b'It all started with one Tweet:\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0just setting up my twttr. Since Twitter launched, our little bird app has become one of the most talked about social platforms. From memes to events to breaking news \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93 Twitter is where it\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s happening and where people are talking about it. Along with a prime spot in the pop culture lexicon, we are prey to some misconceptions about what we do and how we do it. So let\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s break down the common questions and comments we get and talk a little about what is fact vs. myth.'

If you select Not this time, your Tweet will post without an image description.'

=== b'How to add image descriptions' ===

b'You can add image descriptions in four steps.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n      Add image descriptions\n    \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n1.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0After uploading an image to a Tweet, select the +ALT button on the image. (\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cALT\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d is the abbreviation for alternative text, which is the technical name for image description.)\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n2.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Enter a description of the image in the text box. The description for this image is: \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cA small white mug with a tiny loop handle, with a shot of deep brown espresso and a light brown crema on top. The mug sits on a small white saucer on a medium brown wooden table.\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d In the corner of the text box is the character count. We\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ve used 178 characters of the 1,000 characters available.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n3.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Select Done. An ALT badge will appear in the corner of the image. The + symbol no longer appears on the badge now that the description has been added.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n4.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Select Tweet. The ALT badge appears on the image of the posted Tweet. When someone selects the ALT badge, the image description appears on screen from the bottom up.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n1.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0After uploading an image to a Tweet, select the +ALT button on the image. (\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cALT\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d is the abbreviation for alternative text, which is the technical name for image description.)\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n2.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Enter a description of the image in the text box. The description for this image is: \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cA small white mug with a tiny loop handle, with a shot of deep brown espresso and a light brown crema on top. The mug sits on a small white saucer on a medium brown wooden table.\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d In the corner of the screen is the character count. We\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ve used 178 characters of the 1,000 characters available.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n3.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Select Done. An ALT badge will appear in the corner of the image. The + symbol no longer appears on the badge now that the description has been added.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n4.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Select Tweet. When someone selects the ALT badge, the image description appears on screen.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n1. After uploading an image to a Tweet, select Add description underneath the image.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n2. Enter a description of the image in the text box. The description for this image is: "A small white mug with a tiny loop handle, with a shot of deep brown espresso and a light brown crema on top. The mug sits on a small white saucer on a medium brown wooden table." In the corner of the text box is the character count. We\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ve used 178 characters of the 1,000 characters available.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n3.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Select Save. An ALT badge will appear in the corner of the image. (\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cALT\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d is the abbreviation for alternative text, which is the technical name for image description.)\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n4.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Select Tweet. When someone selects the ALT badge, the image description appears on screen.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n      Add multiple images\n    \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nIf you add more than one image to your Tweet on iOS, the images will appear in a horizontal scroll. Select the +ALT badge on each image to add the image descriptions.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nAfter you\'ve added your image descriptions, you\'ll see the ALT badge appear on the images that have a description. People who view your Tweet will be able to select the ALT badge on each image to read the image descriptions.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nIf you add more than one image to your Tweet on Android, the images will appear in a horizontal scroll. Select the +ALT badge on each image to add the image descriptions.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nAfter you\'ve added your image descriptions, you\'ll see the ALT badge appear on the images that have a description. People who view your Tweet will be able to select the ALT badge on each image to read the image descriptions.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nIf you add more than one image to your Tweet, you\'ll see arrows at the top of the dialog that allow you to navigate to each image to add the descriptions.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nSelect Save. After you\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ve added your image descriptions, you\'ll see the ALT badge appear on the images that have a description. A note below the images that says "2 image descriptions" also confirms how many image descriptions have been added.'

=== b'Image description recommendations' ===

b'Writing image descriptions on Twitter is different from writing them elsewhere on the Web in three ways:\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nTwitter has a character limit of 1,000.The description is the only place that guarantees a description of an image.Everyone can access it.\nThe goal of writing image descriptions is to be clear and concise, while giving more context to your Tweet.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Like Tweets, image descriptions must follow the\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Twitter Rules.\nHere\'s a list of recommendations for writing great image descriptions with examples:\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n          Image description recommendations\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n          The List\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\nCapture what\'s importantBe succinct, clear, and detailedBe objectiveWrite out or summarize text in imagesWatch out for acronyms and abbreviationsInclude the image type detailsUse regular sentence structure and letter casingAvoid redundant informationTake care with complex visuals\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n          Details and examples\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n1. Capture what\'s important\nIt\'s important to capture action, movement, relationships, noteworthiness, visual details, and anything unique.\nNote people, pets, things, their names (if relevant), and their relationship to each other. Depending on topic relevance, mention the race, gender, age, etc. of people.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\nCapture what\'s important example\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n1. \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            1. \n          \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThe description for this image could be:\nMy puppy, Beatrix, sits on the left. On the right is the bag of charcoal she just finished shredding. Hunks of charcoal and pieces of the bag are scattered on the floor, along with her red octopus toy.\nThis description is 201 characters long.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n2. Be succinct, clear, and detailed\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nThe character limit for image descriptions is 1,000. Previously, some assistive technology (such as screen readers) stopped reading at 200-250 characters. While this is no longer the case, it\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s still important to be succinct in your description.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nBe succinct, clear, and detailed example\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n2.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            2.\n          \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nAt 224 characters, a long version of this image description could be:\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nA small white mug with a tiny loop handle, with a shot of deep brown espresso and a light brown crema on top. The mug sits on a small white saucer on a medium brown wooden table with clear grain running mostly top to bottom.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nA shorter version, at 137 characters, could be:\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nA shot of espresso with a light brown crema inside a white espresso mug with loop handle. The mug sits on a white saucer on a wood table.\nThe shorter version does it in 87 characters less.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n3.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Be objective\nUnless it\'s an image of yourself, or you know exactly what\'s happening in the image, don\'t editorialize, or make assumptions about what\'s happening. Simply provide enough objective context so readers understand the relevance of the image to your Tweet.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nFor example, if the image is of a politician you don\'t like, don\'t refer to their \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9csilly little face.\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d Say instead that they\'re \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9csmiling, close-lipped into the camera.\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d\n\n\n\n\n\n\nBe objective example\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n3.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            3.\n          \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThe description for this image could be:\nThree smiling men sit on a wicker couch, with no cushions, at the top of a hill covered in packed snow. They\'re wearing winter coats, gloves, wet jeans, and snow-encrusted shoes. A factory looms in the background, and a group of people with sleds are gathered at the bottom of the hill.\nThis description is 298 characters. Instead of saying the men look like they\'re having fun, which is subjective, you can say they\'re smiling. Happiness is implied. Also, it looks like the men in this image are about to couch sled down the hill. They aren\'t actively doing so though. To say that they are is to create a story out of the image, instead of just describing the image.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n4.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Write out or summarize text in images\nIf there\'s text in the image, include it in your description. If it\'s more than 1,000 characters of text, do your best to summarize it, focusing on its relevance to your Tweet.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nIf it\'s a legal document, for example, summarize the content and provide a link to the source in your Tweet, not the image description.\nDepending on what you write in your Tweet, you can exclude certain details from the image description. This also avoids redundancy for readers. For example, if you mention the name of the author and the title of a book in your Tweet, you don\'t need to repeat that information in the image description.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0 \xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\nText in images example\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n4.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            4.\n          \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThe description for this image could be:\nA hand holds open a book of poetry by Mary Oliver called \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cDog Songs.\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d The name of the poem displayed is \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cThe Poetry Teacher.\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d On the opposite page is an illustration of a Beagle laying in the grass. The poem is about how the author negotiated with a university to allow her dog to go with her while she teaches a poetry class.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nThis description is 326 characters. Notice that context was given to the description that does not appear in the image. This is done if that contextual information is not provided in the Tweet.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n5. Watch out for acronyms and abbreviations\nAcronyms should be capitalized. If they\'re not, some screen readers may read them as words, which might not make sense in context. Non-capitalized acronyms may also increase reading difficulty for sighted readers.\nTry to spell out words instead of using abbreviations. Screen readers don\'t always announce them in a meaningful way.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nFor example, with abbreviations like "Dr." for "doctor," some screen readers read each letter instead of reading them as words. So "Dr. Calvin" is read as "d r Calvin." Some people will catch that, or be able to process what it actually means, but others won\'t. The exception is if you\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99re writing out abbreviated text that appears in an image.\nEveryone who reads your description may not know what certain abbreviations mean. Readers who don\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t speak or read the same language may struggle to understand the meaning.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\nAcronyms and abbreviations example\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n5.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            5.\n          \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThe description for this image could be:\nBlack and white photo of two young women walking past Doctor Calvin\'s office, down the brick sidewalk along Lexington Avenue in early December. They\'re bundled up in winter coats.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nThis description is 179 characters. Words that could have been abbreviated are "black and white," "Doctor," "Avenue," and "December." The spelled-out words don\'t detract from the description, nor do they significantly impact the character count.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n6. Include the image type details\nMention if something is a close-up, aerial shot, or black and white photo.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nIf it\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s artwork, describe the type of art: painting, portrait, sculpture, illustration, etc. If there\'s a specific genre associated, add that as well. For example, "anime illustration" instead of just "illustration."\n\n\n\n\n\n\nImage type details example\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n6.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            6.\n          \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThe description for this image could be:\nA view from a hilltop looking down into a valley. Rows of corn stretch from side to side of the photo. The setting sunlight makes the fields look auburn instead of yellow. Beyond the crop rows are softly rising hills, with a few buildings and trees on them. Beyond that are even steeper hills, some shrouded in shadow by long, flat stratus clouds.\nThis description is 347 characters. It\'s a bit long, but hopefully it captures the image contents in an evocative way.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n7. Use regular sentence structure and letter casing\nDescribe the image in complete sentences instead of listing its characteristics. Write in a way that sounds natural or conversational.\nWrite in sentence case instead of all lowercase or ALL CAPS (unless it\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s an acronym or abbreviation).\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSentence structure example\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n7.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            7.\n          \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFor this image, the description could be:\nA view of a slice of the city Sintra, Portugal on an overcast, chilly day. A tour bus is coming down the street, a couple is getting off their scooter, and a group of people are walking toward us. On top of the hill in the distance is Castelo dos Mouros (Castle of the Moors).\nThis description is 276 characters.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n8.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Avoid redundant information\nDon\'t write "Photo of" or "Image of." Assistive technology will know it\'s an image and communicate that to users. Do mention if something is a screenshot. It can be useful for readers to have that extra context.\nDon\'t repeat information that you write in your Tweet in the image description. For example, if you share a photo of a book cover, and mention the author\'s name and book title in your Tweet, don\'t repeat that information in the description; instead describe the book cover. If you don\'t mention that information in your Tweet, then do include it in your description.\n\n\n\n\n\n\nAvoid redundant information example\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n8.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            8.\n          \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThe description for this image could be:\nScreenshot of a Tweet from @Twitter on October 4th that says, \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9chello literally everyone.\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d There were 118,400 comments, 784,200 retweets, and 3.3 million likes.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nThis description is 159 characters. Short and sweet.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n9.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Take care with complex visuals\nDiagrams, charts, tables, maps, and infographics contain detailed information. These visuals often need lengthy image descriptions. The goal for these descriptions is to describe trends and findings, not explain the research behind it. Instead, add a link to the source in your Tweet so readers can get more information if they want it.\nFor maps, describe the overall information shown. No need to describe the interface controls or the pinned landmarks.\n\n\n\n\n\n\nComplex visuals example\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n9.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            9.\n          \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThe description for this image could be:\nScreenshot of 2019 data map from the CDC Disability & Health Data System showing the relationship between any disability and yearly incomes below $15,000 for adults 18+. The states with the highest prevalence of 22.2-50.3% are CA, NM, AR, LA, AL, SC, DC, Guam, and Puerto Rico. States in the second-highest tier of 18.7-22.1% are NE, OK, TX, MO, WI, IN, KY, TN, MS, WV, GA. States in the middle with 17-18.6% are AZ, MT, KS, IL, MI, OH, FL, VA, NY, RI. States in the second-lowest tier of 15.6-16.9% are WA, NV, ID, HI, IA, VT, NH, MA, ME, DE. States with the lowest at 10.2-15.5% are AK, OR, UT, WY, CO, ND, SD, MN, PA, MD, NC. There is no data available for NJ or Virgin Islands. The U.S. median prevalence is 19.7%. The map uses blue and green colors to show percentage relationships in each state.\nThis description is 801 characters, and thorough enough to give readers a comprehensive understanding of the data map.\xc3\x82'

The mug sits on a small white saucer on a medium brown wooden table with clear grain running mostly top to bottom.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nA shorter version, at 137 characters, could be:\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nA shot of espresso with a light brown crema inside a white espresso mug with loop handle. The mug sits on a white saucer on a wood table.\nThe shorter version does it in 87 characters less.\xc3\x82'


=== b'Image description recommendations' ===

b"The description for this image could be:\nThree smiling men sit on a wicker couch, with no cushions, at the top of a hill covered in packed snow. They're wearing winter coats, gloves, wet jeans, and snow-encrusted shoes. A factory looms in the background, and a group of people with sleds are gathered at the bottom of the hill.\nThis description is 298 characters. Instead of saying the men look like they're having fun, which is subjective, you can say they're smiling. Happiness is implied. Also, it looks like the men in this image are about to couch sled down the hill. They aren't actively doing so though. To say that they are is to create a story out of the image, instead of just describing the image."

=== b"What we've done" ===

b"What we've done\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nImage descriptions (alt text)\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nAvailable for still media and GIFsAvailable to everyone, not just assistive technologyImage description reminderALT badge\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nGIF label\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nCaptions\nUpload caption (.srt) filesAutomatic captions (provided by Microsoft) for:Twitter SpacesVoice Tweets\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nHigh-contrast buttons\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nLeft-aligned text\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nWhite background\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSensory guide for Twitter Spaces\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSocial narrative for Twitter Spaces\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nReader - Twitter Blue feature\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nAccessible content labels\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nAccessibility hints for assistive technology\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nKeyboard shortcuts\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSettings\nWebHigh contrast modeReduce motionVideo autoplay on/offFont size customizationDark / Dim modesDisplay color customizationiOSPronounce # as hashtagInclude username in Timeline optionRead shortened URLs optionMagic Tap action to compose TweetHigh contrast modeVideo autoplay on/offOpen links in Reader viewFont size customizationDark / Dim modesMedia previewSound effectsAndroidPronounce # as hashtagReduce motionVideo autoplay on/offMedia previewDark / Dim modesSound effectsFont size customization\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n          What Tweet authors can do\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nWrite great image descriptions.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nWrite in sentence case (instead of all caps or all lowercase).\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nWrite hashtags in camel case (ThisIsCamelCase. Thisisnot.)\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nBreak up large blocks of text with line breaks.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nDon't repeat the same emoji more than 2-3 times, and place them at the end of a sentence.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nAvoid using emoji in your display name.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nUpload a caption file with videos to ensure high-quality, correct captions.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nAvoid special characters. If posting ASCII art, post an image of the art and write an image description of it.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nDon't use ableist language."


=== b'How to use the ALT badge and GIF label' ===

b'The ALT badge\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n"ALT" is the abbreviation for alternative text, which is the technical name for image description. The ALT badge on images lets you know when someone has added a description to their image.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nTo read the image description:\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nSelect the ALT badge and the image description will appear.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nTo exit, select the Dismiss button, escape key, or any spot outside the description. This experience is the same on Android, iOS, and web.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n          The GIF label\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\nThe GIF label is not interactive like the ALT badge. The GIF label communicates that the media is a GIF and has movement. For those who choose to have media auto-play turned off in their timeline, it\'s helpful to have the GIF label to differentiate from static images.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nIf a GIF has an image description, the ALT badge will appear next to it, and you can select it to read the GIF description.\xc3\x82'

=== b'How to upload caption (.srt) file to Tweets' ===

b"Caption files are a specific file type called SRT. SRT stands for Secure Reliable Transport. In addition to writing out all the spoken words and acted content (these are called audio descriptions), each section of captioned text is related to a time window. At that time in your video, the text associated will appear on the screen.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\nHere's an example of what text in a caption file looks like:\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n1\n00:00:05,000 --> 00:00:10,000\nHi, I\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99m Brett Lewis. I\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99m a software\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nEngineer at Twitter with\n2\n00:00:10,000 --> 00:00:15,000\nThe Accessibility Experience Team.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nAnd I\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99m here today as part of\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nRead this article to learn how to create a caption file.\n\n\n\n\nOnce your .srt file is created, here's how to upload it to your Tweet:\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n      How to upload caption (.srt) file to a Tweet\n    \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n1. Upload a video to your Tweet.\n2. Select Upload caption file (.srt)\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0below the video.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n3.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0In the pop-up, select the Upload captions button, then choose the caption file from your computer.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n4. Select Done.\n5. Under the video, the name of the language your captions are written in appears in place of the previous upload command.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n6.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0If you're satisfied with your Tweet text, video, and caption file, select Tweet.\nWhen your video plays, and the viewer has captions enabled, the captions will appear toward the bottom of the video.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nNote: Currently this feature is available on web only.\xc3\x82"


=== b'How to upload caption (.srt) file to Tweets' ===

I\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99m a software\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nEngineer at Twitter with\n2\n00:00:10,000 --> 00:00:15,000\nThe Accessibility Experience Team.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nAnd I\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99m here today as part of\xc3\x82'

If one works and the other does not, it is most likely that the WiFi connection does not accept SSL or is blocking Twitter.\nIf you\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99re connected to a VPN, try turning it off. Clearing data from the app won't remove your account from the app or any of your account information, but it will reset your notification and sync settings to their default settings.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFrom your device's home screen, tap the Settings icon.Select Applications.Select the Twitter app, scroll down and tap Clear Data.If you've cleared your data but are still experiencing the issue, try turning your phone off and then on.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nLog out of your app and log back in\n\nIf clearing your app's data or turning your phone off and then on again didn't work, you should try logging out of the app and then logging back in. Tap whichever icon you have and select Settings and privacy.Tap Account, then tap Log out. This will not deactivate your account, rather this will only log your account out of the app.Confirm the removal of the account by tapping OK.\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nTo log back in to your account\nAfter logging out of the account, you can add it back by opening the app and tapping Log in.Enter your username and password.Tap Log in.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nUninstall and reinstall the Twitter app on your Android device \n\nIf you\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ve enabled login verification on your account, be sure to store a\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0backup code\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0before uninstalling the app.\nLogging out of your account will clear your drafts.\nTo uninstall the Twitter for Android app:\nPlease Note: Before completing the steps below,\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0save any Tweet drafts\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0you\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99d like to keep.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nTo uninstall the Twitter for Android app\nFrom your home screen, press the menu button and select Applications.Select Manage Applications.Select Twitter.Tap the Uninstall icon at the top.If the Twitter for Android app came preloaded on your device, it may not be possible to remove the app completely. If you are unsure of which version you are using, this tool may be able to tell you: https://www.whatsmybrowser.org/.\nInformation on, and downloads of, the latest version of your preferred browser can be found at the links below:\nFirefoxEdgeSafariGoogle Chrome\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nIf a browser upgrade doesn't solve your issue, you can also try downloading an alternate browser using the links above.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nHave you tried clearing your cache and cookies?\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nClearing your browser cache and cookies may resolve the issue. Instructions can be found here:\nClear your browser cacheClear your browser cookies\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nDo you have browser add-ons, plug-ins or extensions installed?\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nSome browser extensions can interfere with actions performed on Twitter.com. Try disabling any browser add-ons you may have enabled (you do not need to delete them completely), which may resolve the issues you are experiencing.\nIf you use any additional software such as an ad-blocker, we'd suggest turning those off one at a time in case our site is being blocked in some way. If you discover the issue is resolved while an application is turned off, you can then troubleshoot with the settings in that software.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nDo you have any third-party connections to your Twitter account?\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nSometimes issues can arise through third-party connections to your Twitter account. Visit your Apps settings to review third-party connections and try revoking access for any unnecessary apps. You can read about how to revoke third-party access to your account.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nLog out of your account \n\nLogging out of your account may help solve the trouble you're experiencing.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nLogging out of your account keeps a draft of your Tweet in the Unsent Tweets section of the Tweet compose box. To find your draft:\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nGo to twitter.comSelect the \n\n\n to open the Tweet compose box.Select Unsent Tweets from the top right corner of the compose box.Select Drafts to find your Tweet.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClear your cache and cookies\n\nClearing your browser cache and cookies may resolve the issue. Instructions can be found here:\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClear your browser cacheClear your browser cookies\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nTurn off browser add-ons, plug-ins or extensions\n\nSome browser extensions can interfere with actions performed on Twitter.com. Try turning off any browser add-ons you may have enabled (you do not need to delete them completely), which may resolve the issues you are experiencing.\nIf you use any additional software such as an ad-blocker, we'd suggest turning those off one at a time in case our site is being blocked in some way. If you discover the issue is resolved while an application is turned off, you can then troubleshoot with the settings in that software.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nRevoke third-party connections to your Twitter account?\n\nSometimes issues can arise through third-party connections to your Twitter account. Visit your\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Apps\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0settings to review third-party connections and try revoking access for any unnecessary apps. You can read about\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0how to revoke third-party access to your account.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n          Share this article\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet"
