=== b'How Black Girl Gamers used Twitter to change the game' ===

b'Over time,\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Black Girl Gamers\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0grew into a bastion for Black women in the industry, whether or not they were a part of our private community. We brought a new lease of life to Diversity & Inclusion narratives in the industry via our vocality and the feeling that \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cenough was enough\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d. We interact with our followers on Twitter, especially our Black women followers because they are the ones who need to be heard and seen the most. They in turn joined the\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0conversation\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0and\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Retweeted\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0us, sending our message out into their own personal communities \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93 a great feature of Twitter. Interacting with our supporters comes naturally. We chat, ask them to teach us, we boost Tweets for good causes, and share jokes with our supporters \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93 we\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99re human and it\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s important to come across as that. This allows us to offer a safe space for discourse (even out in the open).'

=== b'How Black Girl Gamers used Twitter to change the game' ===

b'Diversity and inclusion wasn\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t as \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9ctrendy\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d as it is now and so at times, when Tweeting, I had to step into that \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cangry Black woman\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d label that would be frequently attached to Black Girl Gamers but I didn\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t care. It took thick skin but before I knew it, Retweets on our Tweets calling out publishers would spread our message and our Tweets would often, and still do, have a seat at the table in rooms full of professionals that were too scared to actually speak to or employ Black women directly. Black women from all over the world have come to feel seen by reading our Tweets and appreciate the authenticity in our purpose. We spark and join discussions up until the point of exhaustion or our point being made. And because of this, we still receive messages of thanks for bringing issues to the forefront and using representation in games as the entry point to incite change.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nTwitter is a key part of our strategies for Black Girl Gamers. We receive our best analytics from Twitter, which is due to the massive gamer audience on the platform and the speed at which conversation can spark. The capability to post links in Tweets when promoting events such as our Black Girl Gamers Online Summit and streams with brands like Fortnite, is invaluable to us as a platform. When there are down days (fighting the good fight gets tiring), we Retweet successful content from the past using Twitter\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Media Studio Library\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0or spark lighthearted discussions with our supporters.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Pinning our Tweets\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0keeps our followers up to date on what\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s most important.\nThe visibility of\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Black Girl Gamers\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0has gone through the roof and we still have a way to go. Various members have found us via Twitter to become esteemed and valued members of our Community Management, Stream, or Twitch team. But the visibility isn\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t restricted to just Black women gamers \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93 I once sat in awe of the growth and also our list of verified followers; a far cry from starting a Twitter page to pop off at the industry. Being verified on the platform has also validated our experiences; it\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s shown that we\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99re not to be overlooked in the industry as we were before.\nOur voice has weight.'

=== b'How Black Girl Gamers used Twitter to change the game' ===

b"Our goal is to continue driving change in various areas of gaming; character representation, workforce diversity, inclusion and equity; and become the beacon of Black girl magic that changed the industry for good. We\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ll continue to use Twitter to aid us in our events, workshops, initiatives, and opinions in order to make that change.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nShare this article\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n      ABOUT THE AUTHOR\n    \nJay-Ann is the CEO and Founder of\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Black Girl Gamers\xc3\xa2\xc2\x84\xc2\xa2; an online safe space and platform that heightens the visibility of Black Women in Gaming and advocates for Diversity & Inclusion. In addition to being a global safe space with over 7,000 women, Black Girl Gamers\xc3\xa2\xc2\x84\xc2\xa2 has a following of over 80,000 online and has partnered with V&A Museum, Adidas, Facebook, and Twitch to curate events that highlight the need for inclusion in the industry, including the industry-shaking event Gamer Girls Night In\xc3\xa2\xc2\x84\xc2\xa2. Because of her efforts, Jay-Ann has won several awards and has been requested to speak at Twitter, Unilever, Wellcome Collection, Facebook, and Microsoft on the need for improvement in dominant gaming culture and how companies can do more.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0 She has worked with brands such as Fortnite, MAC, Buildbox, and more to bring visibility and equity to Black Women within the industry.\nJay-Ann is also the Co-Founder of Curlture, a platform boasting over 50,000 followers that empowers women to embrace their natural hair, beauty, and culture via beauty, lifestyle, and travel content. In additional to winning awards as an influencer, Jay-Ann co-authored KINK \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93 a collection of poetry and photography to empower Black women against colourism and texture discrimination. Jay-Ann and her co-founder have been featured on BET, BBC, Channel 4 and worked with Palmers, Harrods Beauty, Paula's Choice, and BET due to their work empowering Black women.\n\n      Follow @jayannlopez_"

b'Conversaciones sobre el derecho al agua en Twitter\n\nEscribo estas l\xc3\x83\xc2\xadneas desde Ayutla Mixe, una comunidad ind\xc3\x83\xc2\xadgena que pertenece al pueblo mixe en las monta\xc3\x83\xc2\xb1as de Oaxaca, en el sur de M\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9xico. En nuestra comunidad y en nuestra cultura la tradici\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3n oral (a la que yo prefiero llamar tradici\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3n mnem\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3nica porque su soporte es la memoria) las palabras son muy importantes. Una gran parte del trabajo cotidiano en nuestros hogares se acompa\xc3\x83\xc2\xb1a de una buena pl\xc3\x83\xc2\xa1tica en mixe, mi lengua materna, en la que abundan an\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9cdotas, historias, preguntas y risas. Ahora que llevo unos a\xc3\x83\xc2\xb1os de haber regresado a vivir en mi comunidad, una de las actividades que m\xc3\x83\xc2\xa1s he extra\xc3\x83\xc2\xb1ado es platicar con personas que est\xc3\x83\xc2\xa1n lejos geogr\xc3\x83\xc2\xa1ficamente.'

b'En febrero de 2010, hace diez a\xc3\x83\xc2\xb1os, abr\xc3\x83\xc2\xad mi cuenta de Twitter, al principio s\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3lo le\xc3\x83\xc2\xad algunas cosas y despu\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9s abandon\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9 la plataforma por mucho tiempo. Sin embargo, poco tiempo despu\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9s, mi cuenta comenz\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3 a ser para m\xc3\x83\xc2\xad un espacio en el que sent\xc3\x83\xc2\xad que podr\xc3\x83\xc2\xada seguir ejercitando el intercambio de palabras y conversaciones que es una actividad muy importante para m\xc3\x83\xc2\xad.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0 Pod\xc3\x83\xc2\xada ponerme a platicar con amigos que se encuentran en otro lugar, personas a las que nunca he conocido f\xc3\x83\xc2\xadsicamente, personas con las que puedo tener afinidades o incluso con otras con las que tengo abiertas y confrontantes diferencias. En Twitter pod\xc3\x83\xc2\xada tambi\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9n plantear ideas de procesos en los que estoy involucrada en la vida real como la lucha por la preservaci\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3n de la diversidad ling\xc3\x83\xc2\xbc\xc3\x83\xc2\xadstica: para ello utilic\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9 Twitter para escribir en mi lengua y dar cuenta de la diversidad en el mundo.'

b'Cuentas como\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0@ActLenguas\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0o\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0@IndigenousTweet, por mencionar s\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3lo un par de ejemplos de los cientos que hay, realizan una gran labor de divulgaci\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3n de la diversidad ling\xc3\x83\xc2\xbc\xc3\x83\xc2\xadstica y me inspirado en ellos. Mi actividad, en ese entonces, se centraba sobre todo en estos temas que me interesan y preocupan. Lamentablemente, en mayo y junio del a\xc3\x83\xc2\xb1o 2017, algo muy lamentable sucedi\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3 en mi comunidad, un grupo violento nos atac\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3 y nos despoj\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3 del manantial del que mi comunidad hab\xc3\x83\xc2\xada tomado agua potable hist\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3ricamente. Nuestra infraestructura hidr\xc3\x83\xc2\xa1ulica, construida con trabajo comunitario, fue completamente destruida; aunado a eso, muchas personas fueron heridas y varias mujeres fueron secuestradas.\nToda la comunidad qued\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3 afectada aunque particularmente la poblaci\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3n infantil y de la tercera edad. La b\xc3\x83\xc2\xbasqueda de justicia por estos hechos y la necesidad de volver a ser conectados a nuestro manantial fue larga y a trav\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9s de distintos medios. La denuncia en Twitter a trav\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9s de los perfiles de las personas que pertenecemos a la comunidad fue uno de esos medios, desde mi cuenta fui narrando las injusticias que est\xc3\x83\xc2\xa1bamos sufriendo y denunciando las amenazas que recibimos cotidianamente. Muchas personas a las que conoc\xc3\x83\xc2\xad virtualmente a trav\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9s de Twitter comenzaron a preguntarme sobre lo que estaba sucediendo en mi comunidad, para conjuntar este tema, comenc\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9 a utilizar el\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0#AguaParaAyutlaYa\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0pues la situaci\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3n se tornaba cada vez m\xc3\x83\xc2\xa1s dif\xc3\x83\xc2\xadcil.\nA principios de mayo de 2019,\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0 a punto de que mi comunidad cumpliera dos a\xc3\x83\xc2\xb1os sin acceso al agua potable, la escritora mexicana Gabriela Ja\xc3\x83\xc2\xbaregui, impuls\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3,\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0 junto a muchas mujeres, la denuncia de la situaci\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3n en la que se encontraba mi comunidad. Lo que sucedi\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3 inmediatamente despu\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9s fue impresionante, much\xc3\x83\xc2\xadsimas cuentas de personas de muy diverso perfil comenzaron a usar el\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0#AguaParaAyutlaYa\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0para ayudar a presionar a las autoridades encargadas de hacer justicia, miles de personas, entre ellas escritores, activistas por los derechos humanos y\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0 periodistas de diferentes medios, se unieron a nuestra causa y a nuestra voz. Derivado de ello, las autoridades locales aceptaron una interlocuci\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3n con nuestra comunidad y nos hemos sentido m\xc3\x83\xc2\xa1s acompa\xc3\x83\xc2\xb1ados en el proceso de b\xc3\x83\xc2\xbasqueda de justicia.'

Con el comienzo de la pandemia de COVID-19, la necesidad del agua se volvi\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3 a\xc3\x83\xc2\xban m\xc3\x83\xc2\xa1s imperante dado que el agua es fundamental para el lavado de manos y as\xc3\x83\xc2\xad lo hemos denunciado tambi\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9n en Twitter.\nDesgraciadamente, a\xc3\x83\xc2\xban no hemos podido lograr la reconexi\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3n a nuestro manantial a pesar de que un juez federal nos ha dado la raz\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3n en el \xc3\x83\xc2\xa1rea legal pero la lucha contin\xc3\x83\xc2\xbaa. A trav\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9s de mi cuenta he dado a conocer lo agradecidos que estamos en nuestra comunidad por todo este gran apoyo que personas que, aunque no conocemos f\xc3\x83\xc2\xadsicamente, nos han ayudado a\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0 denunciar p\xc3\x83\xc2\xbablicamente la situaci\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3n que atravesamos. b"Hablar virtualmente de estos temas tan importantes y tristes para nosotros con m\xc3\x83\xc2\xa1s personas que nos apoyan en nuestra denuncia a trav\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9s de una plataforma como Twitter y por medio del\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0#AguaParaAyutlaYa, nos anima a continuar luchando.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\r\nMuch\xc3\x83\xc2\xadsimas gracias por eso.\n\n\n\n\nShare this article\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n      SOBRE LA AUTORA\n    \nY\xc3\x83\xc2\xa1snaya Elena Aguilar Gil\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0(Ayutla Mixe, 1981) is part of COLMIX, a group of young Mixes that carries out research and dissemination activities on Mixe language, history and culture. She studied Hispanic Language and Literatures and completed a Master's Degree in Linguistics at UNAM. She has collaborated in various projects on the dissemination of linguistic diversity, development of grammatical content for educational materials in Indigenous languages \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x8b\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x8band projects for documentation and attention to languages \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x8b\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x8bat risk of disappearance. === b'Conversations on Twitter about the right to water' ===

b'Ten years ago, I signed up for Twitter. At first, I only spent a little time on the platform and then I left for a while. However, I soon realized that my Twitter account was a space for me to continue exercising in the exchange of words and conversations. This is a vital activity for me. Twitter was and is where I can talk to friends who are elsewhere, with people I have never physically met, and with people I may have affinities with. And even others with whom I have open and confronting differences with. On Twitter, I can also raise ideas around the activism in which I\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99m involved, such as the fight for the preservation of linguistic diversity. For this in particular, I use Twitter to write in my native language and to share an account of the beautiful diversity in our world.'

=== b'Conversations on Twitter about the right to water' ===

b'Accounts like\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0@ActLenguas\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0and\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0@IndigenousTweet\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0are just a couple of examples out of hundreds of accounts that do an amazing job of disseminating linguistic diversity. I\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99m inspired by them. My activism used to focus on all the issues that interested and concerned me. But then in May and June 2017, something very horrific happened in my community. A violent group attacked us and deprived us of the spring from which my community had historically used for drinking water. Our hydraulic infrastructure \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93 built through community work \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93 was completely destroyed. In addition to that, many people were injured and several women were kidnapped.\nOur entire community was affected, but particularly children and the elderly.'


=== b'Conversations on Twitter about the right to water' ===

b'The search for justice for these events and the need to be reconnected to our water source has been a long and painful one. For those of us affected in our community, using Twitter to get the word out was vital.\n\n\nY\xc3\x83\xc2\xa1snaya Elena Aguilar Gil\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet'


=== b'Conversations on Twitter about the right to water' ===

b'From my own account I was narrating the injustices that we were suffering and denouncing the threats we received on a daily basis. Many people I met virtually on Twitter asked me about what was happening in my community, and how they could help. So I began to use\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0#AguaParaAyutlaYa\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0(Water For Ayutla Already) as the situation became increasingly difficult.\n\nIn May 2019, my community was going on two years without access to drinking water. Gabriela Ja\xc3\x83\xc2\xbaregui, a Mexican writer, along with countless women, helped to actively denounce the situation affecting my community. What happened immediately afterwards was impressive: many Twitter accounts from people with incredibly diverse profiles began using\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0#AguaParaAyutlaYa\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0to help put pressure on the authorities in charge of delivering justice to our community. Thousands of people, including writers, human rights activists, and journalists from different media outlets, joined our cause. And our voice. As a result, the local authorities accepted an interlocution with our community. Since then we have felt more seen in the process of seeking justice.'

=== b'Conversations on Twitter about the right to water' ===

b"#AguaParaAyutlaYa\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0has kept the conversation alive around the basic human right to accessing water in our community, and has accompanied our peaceful struggle to achieve justice. Additionally, as we all were confronted by the COVID-19 pandemic, we used Twitter to demand the need for water even louder as water is essential for proper hand washing.\nUnfortunately, we have not yet been able to reconnect to our source despite the fact that a federal judge has agreed with us in legal terms. Nonetheless, our fight continues. Through\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0#AguaParaAyutlaYa\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0I report daily on the news and our progress and through it, people help us to denounce and spread the word that Ayutla still needs water. Our Twitter solidarity is constant, however. We see accounts such as\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0@LeonardoIsaura,\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0@darkolina, and\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0@el_nomad_cook\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0committed to and Tweeting about our struggle.\nA notable Twitter movement from them was on April 15, 2020 \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93 where a call for artists and illustrators to create drawings and illustrations went out to demand\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0#AguaParaAyutlaYa. This call resulted in more than 100 illustrations demanding justice and water for our community and its impact was so tremendous that it caught the attention of various media outlets, such as\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0El Universal\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0and\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0La Jornada. Through my Twitter account, I have expressed how grateful we are in our community. All of this amazing support from people we don\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t personally know offline, yet they've helped us to publicly denounce this horrific situation we are going through."

=== b'Using Twitter to tell it' ===

b'When New Jersey Governor Phil Murphy declared a state of emergency and issued a stay-at-home order, I, like many other Americans, went shopping to stockpile food and necessities. As I saw lines grow and shelves emptied, I decided to make purchases not only for myself, but for my mother and sister. But as I waited for the cashier to bag my items, I thought of the many individuals who did not have the cash on hand to buy items before they were sold out. Or those who did not have a family member to go shopping for them.\n\xc3\x82'


=== b'Using Twitter to tell it' ===

b'It quickly became apparent that COVID-19, like racism, was a virus that was going to disproportionately impact poor and Black and brown communities.\n\n\nZellie Imani\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet'


=== b'Using Twitter to tell it' ===

b'\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nGovernor Phil Murphy\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s stay-at-home order was an important executive order to stop the spread of the deadly coronavirus. But while it may have prevented many from suffering symptoms of COVID-19, it did not prevent communities already suffering from food insecurity. If the goal was for the most vulnerable population to survive the pandemic through self-quarantine, how could they survive if they could not leave their homes to retrieve the groceries, medicine, and necessities to sustain themselves?\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nAround this time, I began seeing activists on my Twitter timeline share sign up sheets to join mutual aid neworks. These networks were quickly popping up all over the country. They were self-organized groups of people sharing resources and supporting neighbors who needed help to survive the pandemic. Recognizing the value in these forms, I did what all good organizers do: I copied it.'

=== b'Using Twitter to tell it' ===

b'As the threat of food insecurity grew, a local IHOP reached out to me, seeking to donate breakfasts. I contacted a local senior home to see if they were able and willing to accept the food donations. I delivered 25 breakfasts for a few days until a senior asked, \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cAre you doing dinner, too?\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d I said, \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cSure.\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d And now, we are delivering 200 dinners, 3 days a week to seniors throughout the city of Paterson.\nAs the demand for the resource grew, so did the need for additional help and funds. By sharing pictures, videos, and our journey on\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Twitter, we began to raise enough money to both expand and continue our operation. People enjoyed the behind the scenes footage of prepping the food and pictures of the seniors we delivered to. We relied heavily on others seeing and sharing our Tweets to raise money to sustain our mutual aid. Posting on Twitter allowed us to garner support from outside our local community, and it quickly became noticed by media outlets who went on to cover our work.'

=== b'Using Twitter to tell it' ===

b'But posting on Twitter wasn\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t simply a way to gain exposure. Twitter has always been a platform to share your life and thoughts with others. There were hundreds of new infections in my city.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Dozens of new deaths. Myself and my team constantly feared we would be next. We shared the good. But we also shared the bad. We constantly discussed shutting down the operation. But each day, we found ourselves back at the restaurant preparing to deliver to seniors that we began to develop bonds with.\nLike the one senior who told me they needed supplies. I called to tell her I purchased them. While on the call she told me she hadn\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t been able to get her medicine. I told her I\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ll pick it up. She said she wanted to hug me, but she can\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t.\nMoments like this meant something to me. But as I shared these moments on Twitter, I learned that it meant something to others as well. It was these moments that were connecting me to strangers online, not simply mutual followers. Twitter is a platform that allows us to share our stories, so my advice to others is, \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cTell it.\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d\nOur efforts taught us that community isn\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t simply about living in proximity to someone, but supporting a fellow human being in times of need. Before the pandemic, many of us had online networks, the pandemic transformed it into online communities. Community is a verb. Community is how we will get through this.\nCommunity is how we will get free.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nShare this article\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n      ABOUT THE AUTHOR\n    \n\nZellie Imani\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0is a writer, educator, and organizer. He is also a co-founder of the Black Liberation Collective, a Black youth Collective dedicated to transforming higher education through unity, coalition building, direct action, and political education.\n\n      Follow @zellieimani'

=== b'Get to know Winnieteca' ===

b'Twittando para democratizar o acesso ao conhecimento : A experi\xc3\x83\xc2\xaancia da Winnieteca\n\nQuando eu era pequena, o mundo visto de dentro da minha casa, parecia muito promissor. Minha av\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3 me ensinava a ler, minha m\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3e dizia o tempo todo o quanto eu era inteligente e especial. Eu corria e ria com as minhas primas e me sentia importante. Minha vida era importante, o que eu pensava era importante e aprender mais para poder pensar mais era estimulado todos os dias.\nOs livros faziam parte de todos os aspectos do meu cotidiano. Tinha livro em todos os lugares da minha casa. Livros de adultos, livros de crian\xc3\x83\xc2\xa7as, livros sobre como as coisas funcionam e livros com hist\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3rias sobre a beleza do mundo. Aprendi meu nome na capa de um desses muitos livros que tinha na minha casa e circundava meu cotidiano. Foi na capa da autobiografia de Winnie Mandela, que reconheci meu nome e a mim mesma.'

=== b'Get to know Winnieteca' ===

b'Contudo, os impactos do racismo no mundo l\xc3\x83\xc2\xa1 fora, n\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3o possibilitavam que minha m\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3e e minha v\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3 me protegessem da viol\xc3\x83\xc2\xaancia racial. Fui para escola e quase sempre era a \xc3\x83\xc2\xbanica crian\xc3\x83\xc2\xa7a negra da minha sala de aula, as vezes a \xc3\x83\xc2\xbanica crian\xc3\x83\xc2\xa7a negra da escola inteira e o que antes era celebra\xc3\x83\xc2\xa7\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3o passou a ser viol\xc3\x83\xc2\xaancia. As brincadeiras racistas dos colegas foram ficando mais frequentes, eu comecei a duvidar de que era inteligente, especial, bonita e importante. Essa viol\xc3\x83\xc2\xaancia racial na escola podia ter significado o meu silencio, poderia ter significado a inviabilidade das minhas potencialidades intelectuais, poderia ter significado o fim do florescimento de uma consci\xc3\x83\xc2\xaancia pol\xc3\x83\xc2\xadtica feminista negra, mas gra\xc3\x83\xc2\xa7as aos livros que circundavam a minha casa, a experi\xc3\x83\xc2\xaancia da viol\xc3\x83\xc2\xaancia racial desde a mais tenra idade me deu a no\xc3\x83\xc2\xa7\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3o de que precisaria resistir.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\xc3\x82'

=== b'Get to know Winnieteca' ===

b'\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nToda vez que eu era violentada racialmente na escola, minha v\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3 me lembrava que o conhecimento \xc3\x83\xc2\xa9 uma das poucas coisas na vida que ningu\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9m pode tirar da gente. Por isso, eu tinha pressa para ler. Lia todos os livros que minha m\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3e trazia, todos os livros da biblioteca da escola, todos os livros que paravam na minha m\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3o. Eu lia e minha av\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3 lia comigo, depois a gente discutia as hist\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3rias. Minha av\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3 me ensinou sobre a import\xc3\x83\xc2\xa2ncia de n\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3o deixar ningu\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9m controlar a nossa pr\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3pria narrativa a partir das conversas sobre as hist\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3rias que l\xc3\x83\xc2\xadamos juntas. Todos os dias eu aprendia uma coisa nova que me ajudava a resistir e todos os dias os livros me proporcionaram pequenas revolu\xc3\x83\xc2\xa7\xc3\x83\xc2\xb5es.\nLer tanto, me proporcionou escrever e nomear minhas pr\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3prias experi\xc3\x83\xc2\xaancias. Nomear as minhas pr\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3prias experi\xc3\x83\xc2\xaancias proporcionou uma compreens\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3o mais ampla sobre as formas de manifesta\xc3\x83\xc2\xa7\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3o do racismo, sobre os estere\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3tipos que s\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3o articulados para manter pessoas negras em lugares de subordina\xc3\x83\xc2\xa7\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3o, sobre as ideologias racistas e sobre as hierarquias que o racismo articula. A leitura me possibilitou conhecimento aut\xc3\x83\xc2\xb4nomo, o conhecimento aut\xc3\x83\xc2\xb4nomo blindou meu intelecto de ser desconstitu\xc3\x83\xc2\xaddo pelas l\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3gicas da viol\xc3\x83\xc2\xaancia racista epist\xc3\x83\xc2\xaamica que atravessa os processos de educa\xc3\x83\xc2\xa7\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3o institucional. A leitura me possibilitou usar a escrita para refletir minha pr\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3pria vez, e o\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Twitter\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0foi a ferramenta onde consegui dizer o que penso e como penso para muitas pessoas ao mesmo tempo.\nEscrever no Twitter\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0sobre meu cotidiano, meus estudos, minhas impress\xc3\x83\xc2\xb5es sobre a sociedade fizeram com que eu constitu\xc3\x83\xc2\xadsse uma rede com milhares de pessoas. O exerc\xc3\x83\xc2\xadcio da influ\xc3\x83\xc2\xaancia no Twitter, entretanto, precisava servir para um prop\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3sito maior que a repercuss\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3o da minha pr\xc3\x83\xc2\xb3pria voz. Eu precisava agir de forma a compartilhar as pequenas revolu\xc3\x83\xc2\xa7\xc3\x83\xc2\xb5es que os livros me proporcionavam.\nNo dia 20 de novembro de 2018, Dia da Consci\xc3\x83\xc2\xaancia Negra no Brasil, a partir de um simples Tweet, eu iniciei uma rede de compartilhamento de livros para pessoas negras. Tudo come\xc3\x83\xc2\xa7ou com uma simples sugest\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3o:\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0ei, pessoas brancas! Que tal FAZER algo para contribuir na luta contra o racismo ao inv\xc3\x83\xc2\xa9s de apenas se auto congratular por se anunciar enquanto antirracista? Que tal doar um livro para uma pessoa negra que precisa de um livro e n\xc3\x83\xc2\xa3o pode comprar?'

b"The Winnieteca experience: Tweeting to democratize access to knowledge\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nHow a\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Direct Message\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0chatbot\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0can change lives\n\r\nWhen I was little, the world from inside my home looked very promising. My grandmother taught me how to read, my mother said all the time how smart and special I was. I played and laughed with my sister and my cousins \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x8b\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x8band I felt important. My life was important, what I thought was important, and learning more and thinking more was encouraged every day.\nBooks were a part of every aspect of my daily life. There was a book everywhere in my house. Adult books, children's books, books about how things work, and books with stories about the beauty of the world. I even learned my name from the cover of one of those many books: Winnie Mandela\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s autobiography,\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Part of My Soul. It was on that cover that I recognized my name and myself."

=== b'Get to know Winnieteca' ===

b'And yet, the impacts of racism on the outside world did not allow my mother and grandmother to protect me from racial violence. I went to school and was almost always the only Black child in my classroom\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93sometimes the only Black child in the entire school. What used to be celebration, became violence. The racist jokes of colleagues became more frequent, and so I started to doubt that I was smart, special, beautiful, and important. This racial violence at school could have meant my silence, it could have meant the infeasibility of my intellectual potentials, it could have meant the end of the flourishing of a Black feminist political conscience, but thanks to the books that had surrounded me in my house, the experience of racial violence from an early age gave me the strength that I would need to resist.\n\xc3\x82'


=== b'Get to know Winnieteca' ===

b'And in order to resist I would need to read.\n\n\nWinnie Bueno\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet'


=== b'Get to know Winnieteca' ===

b"\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nWhenever I was hurt at school, my grandmother reminded me that knowledge is one of the few things in life that no one can take away from us. And that\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s why I had an urge to read. I read all the books my mother bought, all the books in the school library, all the books that I could get my hands on. I read and my grandmother read with me. Then we\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99d discuss the stories. My grandmother has taught me the importance of not letting anyone control our own narrative from conversations we\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99d have about the stories we had read together. Every day I learned something new to help me resist and every day those books gave me small revolutions.\n\r\nReading so much, allowed me to write and name my own experiences. Naming my own experiences has provided a broader understanding of the ways in which racism manifests itself, the stereotypes that are articulated to keep Black people in places of subordination, racist ideologies, and the hierarchies that racism articulates. Reading enabled me to have autonomous knowledge. A knowledge that shielded my intellect from being deconstructed by the logic of epistemic racist violence deep-rooted in the processes of institutional education. Reading made it possible for me to use writing to reflect my own experiences.\nAnd\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Twitter\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0was the tool where I was able to say what I think and how I think to many people at the same time.\nTweeting\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0about my daily life, my studies, and my impressions of society made me form a network with thousands of people. The exercise of influence on Twitter, however, needed to serve a purpose greater than the repercussion of my own voice. I needed to act in order to share the small revolutions that books gave me.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nOn November 20, 2018, Black Awareness Day in Brazil, from a simple\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Tweet, I started a book sharing network for Black people. It all started with a simple suggestion:\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0You know what would be cool to celebrate Black Conscious Day? You, a white privileged person who self congratulates yourself for advertising as an anti-racist, donating a book to a Black person who needs a book and can't buy it."

And she shared her experience on her own profile. Her donations helped people like Gabriela Moura, an amazing Black woman with incredible experience in sharing knowledge and important opinions online.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nWith these first donations until now, this network that I\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99d established became more relevant and impacted more people\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93from the people who donated to the people who received books. We\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ve had support from people like Emicida, a really famous rapper in Brazil, and Gilberto Gil, one of the most important artists in Brazilian musical history. We share books from publishers that help us, we share books from people all around the world who understand the impact of racism in Brazil, and how racism influences educational institutions. We share the gift that I've received since I was young."

=== b'Get to know Winnieteca' ===

b'From a suggestion, I started a network that connects people through books: the\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Winnieteca.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nWinnieteca is a Twitter Direct Message\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0chatbot\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0where Black people who need a book register for the book they need. Then, whoever can donate to the person in need, does so. Winnieteca drives the network of affection and circulation of knowledge that I started with one Tweet, but it\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s sustained by the utopia of a future where access to knowledge and tools to enhance that knowledge\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93such as books\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x93are possible for everyone, everywhere. A future where racism is not a barrier to gain knowledge.'

=== b'About account security' ===

b"To help keep your account secure, we recommend the following best practices:\nUse a strong password that you don\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t reuse on other websites.Use two-factor authentication.Require email and phone number to request a reset password link or code.Be cautious of suspicious links and always make sure you\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99re on twitter.com before you enter your login information.Never give your username and password out to third parties, especially those promising to get you followers, make you money, or verify you.Make sure your computer software, including your browser, is up-to-date with the most recent upgrades and anti-virus software.Check to see if\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0your account has been compromised.\nPassword strength\nCreate a strong and unique password for your Twitter account. You should also create an equally strong and unique password for the email address associated with your Twitter account.\nDo\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s:\nDo\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0create a password at least 10 characters long. Longer is better.Do\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0use a mix of uppercase, lowercase, numbers, and symbols.Do\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0use a different password for each website you visit.Do\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0keep your password in a safe place. Consider using password management software to store all of your login information securely.\nDon\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ts:\nDo not\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0use personal information in your password such as phone numbers, birthdays, etc.Do not\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0use common dictionary words such as \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cpassword\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d, \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9ciloveyou\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d, etc.Do not\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0use sequences such as \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9dabcd1234\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9d, or keyboard sequences like \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9cqwerty.\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x9dDo not\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0reuse passwords across websites. Your Twitter account password should be unique to Twitter.\nAdditionally, you can select\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Password reset protection\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0in your\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Account\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0settings. If you check this box, you will be prompted to enter either your email address or phone number, or your email address then phone number if both are associated with your account to send a reset password link or confirmation code if you ever forget it.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n      How to find your password reset settings\n    \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nNavigate to your main menuTap Settings and privacyTap AccountTap SecurityToggle on Password reset protection\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nNavigate to your App SettingsTap AccountTap SecurityToggle Password reset protection\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nUse two-factor authentication\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\xa8\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\xa8\nTwo-factor authentication is an extra layer of security for your account. Instead of relying on a password only, two-factor authentication introduces a second check to help make sure that you, and only you, can access your Twitter account. Only people who have access to both your password and your mobile phone (or a security key) will be able to log in to your account.\nRead our article on two-factor authentication to learn more.\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\xa8\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\xa8\nCheck that you're on twitter.com\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\xa8 \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\xa8\nPhishing is when someone tries to trick you into giving up your Twitter username, email address or phone number and password, usually so they can send out spam from your account. Often, they\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ll try to trick you with a link that goes to a fake login page. Whenever you are prompted to enter your Twitter password, take a quick look at the URL in the address bar of your browser to make sure you're on twitter.com. Additionally, if you receive a Direct Message (even from a friend) with a URL that looks odd, we recommend you do not open the link.\nPhishing websites will often look just like Twitter's login page, but will actually be a website that is not Twitter. Twitter domains will always have https://twitter.com/ as the base domain. Here are some examples of Twitter login pages:\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\xa8\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0https://twitter.com\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\xa8\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0https://twitter.com/login\nIf you are ever unsure about a login page, go directly to twitter.com and enter your credentials there. If you think you may have been phished, change your password as soon as possible and visit our compromised account article for additional instructions.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nRead about fake Twitter emails for more information about phishing through email.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0 \xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\xa8\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\xa8\nWe won't contact you asking for your password\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\xa8\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\xa8\nTwitter will never ask you to provide your password via email, Direct Message, or reply.\nWe will never ask you to download something or sign-in to a non-Twitter website. Never open an attachment or install any software from an email that claims to be from us; it's not.\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\xa8\nIf we suspect your account has been phished or hacked, we may reset your password to prevent the hacker from misusing your account. In this case, we'll email you a twitter.com password reset link.\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\xa8\nIf you forget your password, you can reset it via this link.\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\nNew and suspicious login alerts\n\n\nIf we detect a suspicious login or when you log in to your Twitter account from a new device for the first time, we will send you a push notification\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0within the Twitter app, or via email as an extra layer of security for your account. Login alerts are only sent following new logins through Twitter for iOS and Android, twitter.com, and mobile web.\nThrough these alerts, you can verify that it was you who logged in from the device. If you did not log in from the device, you should follow the steps in the notification to secure your account, starting by changing your Twitter password immediately. Please note that the location listed in the notification is an approximate location derived from the IP address you used to access Twitter, and it may be different from your physical location.\n\n\n\n\nNote: If you log in to your Twitter account from incognito browsers or browsers with cookies disabled, you will receive an alert each time.\n\n\n\n\nEmail address update alerts\n\n\nAny time the email address associated with your Twitter account is changed, we will send an email notification to the previously-used email address on your account. In the event your account is compromised, these alerts will help you take steps to regain control of your account.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nEvaluating links on Twitter\n\n\nMany Twitter users post links using URL shorteners, like bit.ly or TinyURL, to create unique, shortened links that are easier to share in Tweets. However, URL shorteners can obscure the end domain, making it difficult to tell where the link goes to.\nSome browsers, like Chrome and Firefox, have free plug-ins that will show you the extended URLs without you having to click on them:\n\nURL Expanders for Chrome\nURL Expanders for Firefox\nIn general, please use caution when clicking on links. If you click on a link and find yourself unexpectedly on a page that resembles the Twitter login page, do not enter your username and password. Instead, go to twitter.com and log in directly from the Twitter homepage.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nKeep your computer and browser up-to-date and virus-free\n\n\nKeep your browser and operating system updated with the most current versions and patches\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x94patches are often released to address particular security threats. Be sure to also scan your computer regularly for viruses, spyware, and adware.\nIf you're using a public computer, make sure you sign out of Twitter when you're done.\n\n\nSelect third-party applications with care\n\n\nThere are many third-party applications built on the Twitter platform by external developers that you can use with your Twitter account(s). However, you should be cautious before giving third-party applications access to your account.\nIf you wish to grant a third-party application access to your account, we recommend that you only do so using Twitter\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s OAuth method. OAuth is a secure connection method and doesn\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t require you to give your Twitter username and password to the third party. You should be particularly cautious when you're asked to give your username and password to an application or website, as third-party applications don\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t need your username and password to be granted access to your account via Oauth. When you give your username and password to someone else, they have complete control of your account and can lock you out or take actions that cause your account to be suspended. Learn about connecting or revoking third-party applications.\n\nWe suggest you review third-party applications that have access to your account from time to time. You can revoke access for applications that you don't recognize or that are Tweeting on your behalf by visiting the Applications tab in your account settings.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n          Share this article\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet"

=== b'How to use precise location on mobile devices' ===

b"Delivery of content, including Tweets and advertising, that is better tailored to your location.Delivery of location-specific trends.Showing your followers the location you are Tweeting from as part of your Tweet, if you decide to geotag your Tweet.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n      How to enable and disable location services at the device level\n    \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            Step 1\n          \n\nGo to your device's Settings feature and tap Privacy.\n\n\n\n\n            Step 2\n          \n\nTap Location Services.\n\n\n\n\n            Step 3\n          \n\nNext to Location Services, drag the slider to turn the feature on.\n\n\n\n\n            Step 4\n          \n\nThen, locate the Twitter app in the list and tap Never or While using the app.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            Step 1\n          \n\nGo to your device's Settings feature and tap Apps.\n\n\n\n\n\n            Step 2\n          \n\nLocate Twitter in the list of your apps and tap Permissions, then toggle the switch next to Location to turn on or off.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n      How to enable and disable precise location at the account level within the Twitter app\n    \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            Step 1\n          \n\nIn the top menu, tap your profile icon, then tap Settings and privacy.\n\n\n\n\n            Step 2\n          \n\nTap Privacy and Safety.\n\n\n\n\n            Step 3\n          \n\nUnder Safety, tap Precise location in the Location section.\n\n\n\n\n            Step 4\n          \n\nWithin the Precise location page, drag the slider to turn the feature on or off.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n            Step 1\n          \n\nIn the top menu, you will either see a navigation menu icon\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n or your profile icon. Tap whichever icon you have, then tap Settings and privacy.\n\n\n\n\n            Step 2\n          \n\nTap Privacy and Safety.\n\n\n\n\n            Step 3\n          \n\nUnder Safety, tap Precise location in the Location section.\n\n\n\n\n            Step 4\n          \n\nWithin the Precise location page, tap the checkbox to turn the feature on or off.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n          Share this article\n        \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet"


=== b'Tweet location FAQs' ===

b'What location information is attached to my Tweets?\r\n \xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nEnabling precise location allows you to selectively add location information to your Tweets. This feature is off by default and you will need to opt in to use it.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0This allows Twitter to collect, store, and use your precise location, such as GPS information.\nOnce you\'ve enabled precise location, you will be able to attach a location (such as a city or neighborhood) of your choice to your Tweet. Simply tap the location marker while composing your Tweet, and select the location you wish to tag.\nNote: Once you Tweet with a location, your next Tweet will automatically include a general location label. Learn how to turn location off at any time.Third-party applications or websites may let you Tweet with location, including your precise location. We ask these developers to clearly explain what information is being shared when you use their products to Tweet with location.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nWhat controls do I have when I attach location information to my Tweets?\r\n \xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nEven after you enable Tweeting with your location, you have additional control over which Tweets (and what type of location information) is shared. With this in mind:\nTweet location is off by default, and you will need to opt in to the service.\nYou can turn Tweet location on or off at any time.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0You can delete your past location data from displaying in your Tweets in a single place (see this article for step-by-step instructions).Be cautious and careful about the amount of information you share online. There may be some updates where you want to share your location ("The parade is starting now" or "A truck just spilled delicious candy all over the roadway!"), and some updates where you want to keep your location private. Just like you might not want to Tweet your home address, please be cautious when Tweeting from locations that you don\'t want others to see.Remember that when you\'re opted into Tweet location, suggested locations may be offered to you, but you can still choose not to share your location for individual Tweets (see this article for instructions).Please familiarize yourself with our general location settings and the settings of any applications and devices you Tweet with so that you are always aware of the information you share.Remember, once you post something online, it\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s out there for others to see.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nWhat location information is displayed?\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nAll geolocation information begins as a location (latitude and longitude), sent from your browser or device. Twitter won\'t show any location information unless you\'ve opted in to the feature, and have allowed your device or browser to transmit your coordinates to us.If you have chosen to attach location information to your Tweets, your selected location label is displayed underneath the text of the Tweet.On twitter.com, you can select a location label such as the name of a neighborhood or city.When you use the in-app camera on Twitter for iOS and Android to attach a photo or video to your Tweet\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0and toggle on the option to tag your precise location, that Tweet will include both the location label of your choice and your device\'s precise location (latitude and longitude), which can be found via API. Your precise location may be more specific than the location label you select.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0This is helpful when sharing on-the-ground moments.\nNote:\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0The option to share your precise location from the in-app camera is currently available only on newer versions of Twitter for iOS (6.26 or later) and on newer versions of Twitter for Android (version 5.55 or later).\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0Application developers are required to be up-front and obvious about whether your exact coordinates, or just the place, will be included in your Tweet. When you Tweet from a third-party application or mobile device, it should be clear which type of data will be included in your Tweet.\n\n\n\n\nNote: In some areas, you have the option to label your Tweet with a specific business, landmark, or point of interest. These places are sourced from Foursquare. If you see an issue with a place, please report it via Foursquare\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s Help Center. If you believe that a specific Tweet is abusive, please report it to Twitter.'

=== b'Report impersonation accounts' ===

b"Impersonation is a violation of the Twitter Rules. Accounts\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0that pose as another person, group, or organization in a confusing or deceptive manner may be permanently suspended under Twitter\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s misleading and deceptive identities policy.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nHow do I report an impersonation violation?What happens when Twitter receives a valid report?Can I request a specific username?Someone is using my email address, what can I do?What if my company is being impersonated or my trademarked brand is being misused?\n\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\nHow do I report an impersonation violation?\n\n\nIf you believe an account is posing as you or your brand, you or your authorized representative can file a report in our Help Center.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nIf you believe an account is misusing the identity of somebody else, you can flag it as a bystander by reporting directly from the account\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s profile.\nYou do not need a Twitter account to report impersonation on Twitter.\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\r\n What happens when Twitter receives a valid report?\n\n\nUpon receipt of an impersonation report, we will investigate the reported account to determine if\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0it violates the Twitter Rules. Accounts determined to be in violation of our\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0misleading and deceptive identities policy, or those not in compliance with our parody, commentary, and fan account policy, will either be suspended or asked to update the account(s) so they no longer violate our policies.\nReporting an impersonation account is separate from account verification. Read more about verified accounts.\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\nCan I request a specific username?\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\r\n \xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nWe generally do not accept individual requests for inactive or suspended usernames.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\nSomeone is using my email address, what can I do?\n\n\nAre you trying to create a new account, but you're told your email address or phone number is already in use? This support article outlines how your email address may already be in use\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0and how to resolve the issue.\n\n\n\n\xc2\xa0\n\n\n\n\nWhat if my company is being impersonated or my trademarked brand is being misused?\n\n\nCompanies and businesses should report accounts misusing their trademarks or brand by filing a complaint under our trademark policy. Please review the Trademark Policy page, as there is specific information we will need to process your claim."


=== b'About fake Twitter emails' ===

b"Twitter will only send you emails from @twitter.com or @e.twitter.com. However, some people may receive fake or suspicious emails that look like they were sent by Twitter. These emails might include malicious attachments or links to spam or phishing websites. Please know that Twitter will never send emails with attachments or request your Twitter password by email.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nIf you receive a fake email\n\n\nDelete the email from your inbox. Don't download any attachments from these emails.Find more account security tips in our Help Center.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nFrequently asked questions\n\nWhat's phishing?\n\nPhishing scammers send fraudulent messages to a large number of people, in an attempt to trick them into revealing private information, like a password. An email or website may be disguised to appear legitimate.\nIt can be difficult to recognize a spoofed email as they may look very convincing or appear to come from a Twitter email address. You can check the headers of an email to find out more about the source of the message, and you should be suspicious of new or unexpected emails. Twitter doesn't send emails with attachments, and will never ask you to provide your password via email, Direct Message, or reply.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nWhat if I'm worried that someone has access to my Twitter username and password?\r\n \xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nIf you suspect your account has been compromised, you can find out what to do on our compromised accounts help page.\nIf Twitter believes your account has been hacked, we may reset the account password to prevent the hacker from misusing your account. In this case, we'll email you a secure link to where you can select a new password. Again, this link will always be on the https://twitter.com website, and we never ask you to provide your password via email, Direct Message, or reply.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nWhy am I getting these fake emails?\n\n\nTwitter doesn't send these emails. The FTC has a help page that describes some ways spammers may find your email address: https://www.consumer.ftc.gov/.\nFor more information about Twitter's policies on information collection, as well as disclosure and sharing, please visit our privacy page at https://twitter.com/privacy."


=== b'About offensive content' ===

b'Twitter is a social broadcast network that enables people and organizations to publicly share brief messages instantly around the world. This brings a variety of people with different voices, ideas, and perspectives. People are allowed to post content, including potentially inflammatory content, as long as they\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99re not violating the Twitter Rules. It\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s important to know that Twitter does not screen content or remove potentially offensive content.\nAs a policy, we do not mediate content or intervene in disputes between users. However, targeted abuse or harassment may constitute a violation of the Twitter Rules and Terms of Service. If you are a victim of targeted abuse or harassment, read more about online abuse.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nHave you seen something on Twitter you disagree with? Here are some tips that may help you deal with your situation:\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nConsider the context\r\n \xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nTwitter lets us participate in broad conversations and connect with people from many corners of the world. While hearing from more people can be enriching, it can also be a source of frustration and misunderstanding if the context of the conversation is not considered. Seeing your username mentioned in a Tweet can be confusing if you don\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t understand why it was used.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nWhen you see an upsetting Tweet, step back and consider the larger conversation it may be connected to. Since individual Tweets are short, the author\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s intended meaning may have been lost or distorted. Tweet back with a reply\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0to join the conversation and surface the concern. Send a Direct Message if you would prefer to communicate privately. Having more information makes it easier to understand the context and can lead to healthy dialogue.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nThink before you Tweet\r\n \xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nHealthy conversation is a shared responsibility.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0If your Tweet reply is identified as using potentially harmful or offensive language, we may ask you, via a prompt, if you want to review it before sending. There will be options to send, edit, or delete the Tweet reply. And if you think we make a mistake, you can let us know.\nNote: These prompts are only available to people using Twitter in English.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nBlock and ignore\r\n \xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nUnderstanding the context often diffuses a negative or confusing interaction, but, there are times when further action, like unfollowing or blocking someone, may be more effective. When you block, you will not be notified when they mention you, Retweet you, like your content, add you to a list or follow one of your lists. You also won\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t see any of these interactions in your timeline.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nFor more information on how to manage a situation that you believe is abusive, read this article about online abuse.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nThere are also many online safety resources\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0that can help.\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\xc3\x82'


=== b'About age screening on Twitter' ===

b'What is age screening?\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nAge screening is a way for brands and others to determine online whether a follower meets a minimum age requirement, in a way that is consistent with relevant industry or legal guidelines. This makes it easier for advertisers and others with content not suitable for minors (e.g. alcohol advertisers) to advertise on Twitter.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nHow does age screening work on Twitter?\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nTwitter has developed a solution for brands that requires new Twitter followers to enter their birth date before being permitted to follow their account. If you have already entered your date of birth on your profile page, it will be detected and you will be able to immediately follow the account. If you have not already entered your date of birth on your profile page, we will ask you to enter your date of birth on your profile page settings.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nThe feature was designed to help brands determine whether a follower meets a minimum age requirement, while at the same time providing an easy and secure way for you to follow accounts that you would otherwise be blocked from following. Twitter advertisers who use the solution will not have access to your birthdate or age unless your birthday visibility settings permit them to view this information on your profile, but will know when you\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ve entered an age that\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s above their indicated threshold. This feature is free, and available to a select number of our advertising partners.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nDoes age screening comply with applicable guidelines and best practices?\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nCompliance with specific industry guidelines around age screening and age-based targeting is the responsibility of the brand.'


=== b'What to do about self-harm and suicide concerns on Twitter' ===

b'If you or someone you know is struggling or in crisis, you\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99re not alone. Use the contact info below to get help.\nUnited States: Contact the National Suicide Prevention Lifeline at 988. Crisis workers are available 24 hours a day. Calls are free and confidential.Other countries & regions: To find a crisis center near you, visit International Association for Suicide Prevention.\nIf you or someone you know is thinking about engaging in self-harm or suicidal behavior, you should seek help as soon as possible by contacting services with expertise in crisis intervention and suicide prevention. You can also alert the Twitter team focused on handling reports associated with accounts that may be engaging in self-harm or suicidal behavior if you encounter this type of content on Twitter.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nTwitter\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99s approach to content associated self-harm and suicide threats\r\n \xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nAfter receiving a report of someone who may be thinking about self-harm or suicide, Twitter will contact the affected individual to let them know that someone who cares about them identified that they might be at risk of harm. We will also encourage them to seek support, and provide information about dedicated online and hotline resources that can help.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nRecognize the signs\r\n \xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nJudging behavior based on online posts alone is challenging, but there are potential warning signs or indicators that someone may be thinking about\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0 self-harm or suicide. Below are questions that you may ask yourself to help assess if an individual may be experiencing suicidal thoughts:\nDoes this person frequently post content about depression or feelings of hopelessness?\nIs this person posting comments about death or feelings that death is the only option?\nAre they posting comments about having attempted suicide in the past?\nAre they describing or posting photos of self-harm or identifying themselves as suicidal?\nHas their mood and the content of their posts changed recently?\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\n\nIf you are concerned and know the person involved, it can be helpful to contact them personally\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0 and encourage them to seek advice from dedicated services who may be able to help. If, on the other hand, you don\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t know the person involved, you may still choose to contact them to express concern or refer them to dedicated organizations , a suicide hotline, or someone who might know them personally. If you don\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t feel comfortable reaching out to the person on your own or aren\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t sure how to reach them, you can also alert Twitter via our dedicated reporting flow.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nManaging experiences with self-harm or suicidal thoughts\r\n \xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nIf you are thinking about engaging in self-harm or suicidal behavior, or are experiencing feelings of depression or anxiety, it may help to talk to people that you trust or to connect with dedicated organizations who can provide support and assistance to help manage these experiences.\nDepression has a wide variety of symptoms and affects millions of people every year. Common symptoms include sadness, loss of interest in activities, changes in appetite and sleep patterns, loss of energy, difficulty thinking, and possibly thoughts of suicide. You might exhibit these types of behaviors, or they might be subtler. Either way, don\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t ignore them.\n\xc3\x82'


=== b'About online abuse' ===

b'Being the target of online abuse and bullying is not easy to deal with. Knowing the appropriate steps to take to address your situation can help you through the process.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nWhen to report it?\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nWe\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99ve all seen something on the Internet we disagree with or have received unwanted communication. Such behavior does not necessarily constitute online abuse and cyberbullying. If you see or receive a reply you don\xc3\xa2\xc2\x80\xc2\x99t like, unfollow and end any communication with that account.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nIf the behavior continues, it is recommended that you block the account. Blocking will prevent that person from following you, seeing your profile image on their profile page, or in their timeline; additionally, their replies or mentions will not show in your Notifications tab (although these Tweets may still appear in search).\nAbusive accounts often lose interest once they realize that you will not respond. If the account in question is a friend, try addressing the issue offline. If you have had a misunderstanding, it may be possible to clear the matter up face to face or with the help of a trusted individual.\nIf you continue receiving unwanted, targeted and continuous replies on Twitter, and feel it constitutes online abuse, consider reporting the behavior to Twitter.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nTake threats seriously\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nIf you believe you are in physical danger, contact the local law enforcement authorities who have the tools to address the issue.\nIf you decide to work with law enforcement, make sure to do the following:\nDocument the violent or abusive messages with print-outs or screenshots\nBe as specific as possible about why you are concernedProvide any context you have around who you believe might be involved, such as evidence of abusive behavior found on other websitesProvide any information regarding previous threats you may have received\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nYou can report the content to Twitter here.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nReach out to the people you trust\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nWhen dealing with negative or hurtful interactions, it can help to turn to family and friends for support and advice. Oftentimes, talking with your relatives or a close friend may help you figure out how you want to handle the situation or let you express your feelings so you can move on.\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nHelp others\r\n\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nTrying to figure out how to help someone in such a situation can be daunting. This Twitter Support article offers some suggestions for how to help a friend or family member with online abuse.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nIf you see a violent or abusive message directed at someone else, communicate your concern to the recipient and encourage them to contact Twitter and their local authorities.\xc3\x82\xc2\xa0\nThere are also many online safety resources that can help.'
